I want to warn you now that this is long:\r\n\r\nWe are pleased to announce our third annual Fashion Campus NYC program!\r\n\r\nParsons the New School For Design and the New York City Economic Development Corporation (NYCEDC) launched Fashion Campus NYC in 2011 to expose students to the variety of business-related career paths in NYC\u2019s fashion industry. This complimentary program continues to evolve, attracting an increasingly global group of participants as well as more New York fashion companies with each passing year.\r\n\r\nThis year Fashion Campus NYC will take place over three evenings starting Monday, July 22, through Wednesday, July 24, 2013.\r\n\r\nEvent highlights include:\r\n\r\nA keynote speech from a top fashion executive\r\nA peer panel discussion featuring young professionals working on the business side of the industry\r\nA networking social with fashion executives and human resource managers (previous employer participants include Aeropostale, American Eagle, Calvin Klein, Coach, Elie Tahari, Gilt Groupe, John Varvatos, Lord & Taylor, Macy\u2019s, Polo Ralph Lauren, Saks Fifth Avenue)\r\nSmall-group workshop sessions organized by career path\r\n\r\nIn order to apply, see requirements below:\r\n\r\nUndergraduate students must:\r\n\r\nHave a for-credit or paid internship in NYC this summer\r\n\r\nBe a rising college/university junior or senior in good standing\r\n\r\nHave at least a 3.0 GPA\r\n\r\nBe able to attend all of the program\u2019s events\r\n\r\n\r\nMBA and Graduate students must:\r\n\r\nBe in good standing in an MBA or graduate program in business or a related field\r\n\r\nHave an internship, fellowship, or similar in a business field in NYC this summer\r\n\r\nBe able to attend all of the program\u2019s events\r\n\r\nPlease note: Fashion Campus NYC focuses exclusively on the business of fashion and is not geared toward design or journalism. Our goal is to educate participants on disciplines such as buying and planning, merchandising, product development, PR/marketing, sales and e-commerce. Space is limited, so we encourage early applications. Please note the application deadline is June 28th.\r\n\r\nWe have attached this announcement and a flyer for you to share with potential applicants. So many of our partners and friends in the educational community were instrumental in spreading the word about last year\u2019s event, so we seek your support in becoming an ambassador to Fashion Campus NYC.
